\DoxyCodeLine{16 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{17 \textcolor{comment}{    PLEASE READ}}
\DoxyCodeLine{18 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{19 \textcolor{comment}{    These root certificates here are included just to make the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{20 \textcolor{comment}{    SSL client examples work. They are NOT intended to be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{21 \textcolor{comment}{    illustrative of best-\/practices for performing TLS certificate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{22 \textcolor{comment}{    verification.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{23 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{24 \textcolor{comment}{    A REAL program which needs to verify the authenticity of a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{25 \textcolor{comment}{    server IP address resolved from a given DNS name needs to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{26 \textcolor{comment}{    consult the operating system specific certificate store}}
\DoxyCodeLine{27 \textcolor{comment}{    to validate the chain of signatures, compare the domain name}}
\DoxyCodeLine{28 \textcolor{comment}{    properly against the domain name in the certificate, check}}
\DoxyCodeLine{29 \textcolor{comment}{    the certificate revocation list, and probably do some other}}
\DoxyCodeLine{30 \textcolor{comment}{    things.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{31 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{32 \textcolor{comment}{    ALL of these operations are entirely outside the scope of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{33 \textcolor{comment}{    both Boost.Beast and Boost.Asio.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{34 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{35 \textcolor{comment}{    See (work in progress):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{36 \textcolor{comment}{        https://github.com/djarek/certify}}
\DoxyCodeLine{37 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{38 \textcolor{comment}{    tl;dr: root\_certificates.hpp should not be used in production code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{39 \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{40 }
